- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 001 "Minto Pyramid Writing Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the doctrine assumes a reader-directed document with a decision or action at stake, and free-form creative prose sits outside its warrant

## Section 011: Decision Tradeoff Guide
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed guide keys adopt, adapt, and avoid to generic evidence agreement instead of this theme's variables, decision stakes, answer clarity, reader position, and medium
- **supporting_reason:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the doctrine binds hardest where a reader must decide, and the source itself relaxes it, use the SCQA flow even if the final prose will imply part of it
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: judging answer clarity is subjective, a writer who believes the answer is clear may still fail the one-sentence test
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: the guide calibrates doctrine strictness per document and cannot waive the six core rules where structure is claimed
- **revision_decision:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to rekey adopt to full workflow for decision documents and decks, adapt to implied SCQA and shallow trees for short or informal pieces, and avoid to reference docs and exploratory notes where no reader question exists

## Section 018: Workload Model
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed model bounds endpoints per batch but not this theme's working unit, one document's pyramid built and validated per focused pass, with depth as the real cost driver
- **supporting_reason:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the workflow expands one level at a time and each level multiplies the question-answer work, so effort scales with tree depth and width rather than page count
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: depth-based bounds are estimates, a shallow document with contested analysis can outweigh a deep routine one
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: the model bounds structuring work per session and does not bound the prose-drafting effort that follows
- **revision_decision:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to rebound the model around one document per pass, Key Line plus one level as the default depth, and the bottom-up regrouping pass budgeted separately when the answer starts fuzzy
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the expensive case is the fuzzy answer, the bottom-up pass is unbounded grouping work with no guaranteed convergence, so answer clarity at calibration is the best single workload predictor

## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed bullets classify verification failures generically and never carry this theme's retry rule, a failed structure is rebuilt at the failing level, not re-polished at the surface
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the doctrine's repairs are level-specific, the bottom-up pass for fuzzy answers, regrouping for unnameable classes, reordering for arbitrary sequence, so retries must target the diagnosed level
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: level-targeted retries assume correct diagnosis, a misread defect sends the rework to the wrong layer
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: this governs both retrying document structure and retrying reference-verification work, kept as two labeled layers
- **revision_decision:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to add the writing-layer rule, retries must change the failing level, recalibrate for wrong questions, regroup for mixed siblings, reorder for arbitrary sequence, and never respond to structural failure with prose polish
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that prose polish is this theme's retry-without-change, it alters the surface while reproducing the structure, which is why the overview commands fixing structure before polishing prose

## Section 023: Performance Verification Method
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

- **supporting_reason:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the doctrine claims structure work up front saves rework later, a claim testable by comparing first-pass checklist yield between structured and unstructured drafts
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: editorial comparisons confound author skill with method, and small document counts make trends noisy
